namespace = DG_Hellenic
country_event = { 
	id = DG_Hellenic.001
	title = "DG_Hellenic.001.title"
	desc = "DG_Hellenic.001.desc"
	picture = hellenic_oracle
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Hellenic.001.opta"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 20
			modifier = { 
				is_at_war = yes
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { 
				is_at_war = no
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			set_country_flag = oracle_war
		}
		random_list = { 
			60 = { 
				country_event = { 
					id = DG_Hellenic.002
					days = 30
				}
			}
			40 = { 
				country_event = { 
					id = DG_Hellenic.003
					days = 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Hellenic.001.optb"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 20
			modifier = { 
				is_at_war = yes
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { 
				is_at_war = no
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = { 
				NOT = { 
					num_of_generals = 1
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { 
				NOT = { 
					army_tradition = 10
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { 
				NOT = { 
					army_tradition = 25
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { 
				army_tradition = 90
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = { 
				army_tradition = 75
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = { 
				army_tradition = 50
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = { 
				num_of_generals = 1
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = { 
				num_of_generals = 2
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = { 
				num_of_generals = 3
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			set_country_flag = oracle_general
			random_list = { 
				60 = { 
					country_event = { 
						id = DG_Hellenic.002
						days = 30
					}
				}
				40 = { 
					country_event = { 
						id = DG_Hellenic.003
						days = 30
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Hellenic.001.optc"
		trigger = { 
			government = monarchy
			has_heir = no
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 20
			modifier = { 
				is_at_war = no
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			set_country_flag = oracle_heir
			random_list = { 
				60 = { 
					country_event = { 
						id = DG_Hellenic.002
						days = 30
					}
				}
				40 = { 
					country_event = { 
						id = DG_Hellenic.003
						days = 30
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Hellenic.001.optd"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 20
			modifier = { 
				is_at_war = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = { 
				is_bankrupt = yes
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			set_country_flag = oracle_invest
			random_list = { 
				60 = { 
					country_event = { 
						id = DG_Hellenic.002
						days = 30
					}
				}
				40 = { 
					country_event = { 
						id = DG_Hellenic.003
						days = 30
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Hellenic.001.opte"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 20
			modifier = { 
				num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { 
				num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 2
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { 
				NOT = { 
					stability = 0
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { 
				NOT = { 
					stability = -1
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { 
				NOT = { 
					stability = -2
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { 
				stability = 1
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = { 
				stability = 2
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = { 
				stability = 3
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			set_country_flag = oracle_peace
			random_list = {

	}

country_event = { 
	id = DG_Hellenic.002
	title = "DG_Hellenic.002.title"
	desc = "DG_Hellenic.002.desc"
	picture = hellenic_oracle
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { 
		hidden_effect = { 
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					ai = yes
				}
				random_list = { 
					70 = { 
						set_country_flag = oracle_good_advice
					}
					30 = { 
						set_country_flag = oracle_bad_advice
					}
				}
			}
			else = { 
				random_list = { 
					60 = { 
						set_country_flag = oracle_good_advice
					}
					40 = { 
						set_country_flag = oracle_bad_advice
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Hellenic.002.opta"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 75
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				monthly_income = 500
			}
			add_treasury = -500
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				monthly_income = 10
			}
			add_years_of_income = -0.08
		}
		else = { 
			add_treasury = -10
		}
		country_event = { 
			id = DG_Hellenic.005
			days = 100
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Hellenic.002.optb"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 25
		}
		add_prestige = -1
		hidden_effect = { 
			clr_country_flag = oracle_war
			clr_country_flag = oracle_general
			clr_country_flag = oracle_heir
			clr_country_flag = oracle_invest
			clr_country_flag = oracle_peace
			clr_country_flag = oracle_good_advice
			clr_country_flag = oracle_bad_advice
		}
	}
}
country_event = { 
	id = DG_Hellenic.003
	title = "DG_Hellenic.003.title"
	desc = "DG_Hellenic.003.desc"
	picture = hellenic_oracle
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Hellenic.003.opta"
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				DIP = 6
			}
			add_legitimacy = 4
			add_devotion = 8
			add_republican_tradition = 2
			add_prestige = 4
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				DIP = 5
			}
			add_legitimacy = 3
			add_devotion = 6
			add_republican_tradition = 1.5
			add_prestige = 3
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				DIP = 4
			}
			add_legitimacy = 2
			add_devotion = 4
			add_republican_tradition = 1
			add_prestige = 2
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				DIP = 3
			}
			add_legitimacy = 1
			add_devotion = 2
			add_republican_tradition = 0.5
			add_prestige = 1
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				DIP = 1
			}
			add_legitimacy = -1
			add_devotion = -2
			add_republican_tradition = -0.5
			add_prestige = -1
		}
		else = { 
			add_legitimacy = -2
			add_devotion = -4
			add_republican_tradition = -1
			add_prestige = -2
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			clr_country_flag = oracle_war
			clr_country_flag = oracle_general
			clr_country_flag = oracle_heir
			clr_country_flag = oracle_invest
			clr_country_flag = oracle_peace
		}
	}
}
country_event = { 
	id = DG_Hellenic.004
	title = "DG_Hellenic.004.title"
	desc = "DG_Hellenic.004.desc"
	picture = hellenic_philosophy
	trigger = { 
		religion = hellenic_pagan
		OR = { 
			has_regency = no
			has_consort_regency = yes
		}
		NOT = { 
			has_ruler_modifier = cynicism_philosophy
		}
		NOT = { 
			has_ruler_modifier = epicurianism_philosophy
		}
		NOT = { 
			has_ruler_modifier = stoicism_philosophy
		}
		NOT = { 
			has_country_flag = hellenistic_philosophies_neutral
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		years = 10
		modifier = { 
			is_at_war = yes
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = { 
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = { 
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = { 
			NOT = { 
				piety = -0.20
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = { 
			NOT = { 
				piety = -0.60
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
	}
	immediate = { 
		hidden_effect = { 
			set_country_flag = hellenistic_philosophy
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Hellenic.004.opta"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10
			modifier = { 
				any_known_country = { 
					overlord_of = ROOT
					has_ruler_modifier = cynicism_philosophy
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { 
				NOT = { 
					prestige = 0
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = { 
				prestige = 25
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = { 
				prestige = 50
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = { 
				prestige = 75
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = { 
				prestige = 100
				factor = 0.7
			}
		}
		add_ruler_modifier = { 
			name = "cynicism_philosophy"
		}
		every_country = { 
			limit = { 
				religion = hellenic_pagan
				has_ruler_modifier = cynicism_philosophy
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					piety = 0.6
				}
				add_opinion = { 
					who = ROOT
					modifier = same_doctrine_fanatical
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					piety = 0.2
				}
				add_opinion = { 
					who = ROOT
					modifier = same_doctrine_pious
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					piety = -0.2
				}
				add_opinion = { 
					who = ROOT
					modifier = same_doctrine_observant
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Hellenic.004.optb"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 30
			modifier = { 
				any_known_country = { 
					overlord_of = ROOT
					has_ruler_modifier = epicurianism_philosophy
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { 
				government = republic
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = { 
				government = monarchy
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = { 
				NOT = { 
					stability = 0
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = { 
				num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = { 
				is_at_war = yes
				factor = 0.7
			}
		}
		add_ruler_modifier = { 
			name = "epicurianism_philosophy"
		}
		every_country = { 
			limit = { 
				religion = hellenic_pagan
				has_ruler_modifier = epicurianism_philosophy
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					piety = 0.6
				}
				add_opinion = { 
					who = ROOT
					modifier = same_doctrine_fanatical
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					piety = 0.2
				}
				add_opinion = { 
					who = ROOT
					modifier = same_doctrine_pious
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					piety = -0.2
				}
				add_opinion = { 
					who = ROOT
					modifier = same_doctrine_observant
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Hellenic.004.optc"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 20
			modifier = { 
				any_known_country = { 
					overlord_of = ROOT
					has_ruler_modifier = stoicism_philosophy
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { 
				government = republic
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = { 
				num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		add_ruler_modifier = { 
			name = "stoicism_philosophy"
		}
		every_country = { 
			limit = { 
				religion = hellenic_pagan
				has_ruler_modifier = stoicism_philosophy
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					piety = 0.6
				}
				add_opinion = { 
					who = ROOT
					modifier = same_doctrine_fanatical
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					piety = 0.2
				}
				add_opinion = { 
					who = ROOT
					modifier = same_doctrine_pious
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					piety = -0.2
				}
				add_opinion = { 
					who = ROOT
					modifier = same_doctrine_observant
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "DG_Hellenic.004.optd"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 40
			modifier = { 
				NOT = { 
					primary_culture = greek
				}
				factor = 2
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { 
	id = DG_Hellenic.005
	title = DG_Hellenic.005.t
	desc = DG_Hellenic.005.d
	picture = all_powerful_advisor
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { 
		hidden_effect = { 
			random_list = { 
				50 = { 
					set_country_flag = oracle_first_option
				}
				50 = { 
					set_country_flag = oracle_second_option
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = DG_Hellenic.005.a
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = oracle_war
				has_country_flag = oracle_good_advice
				has_country_flag = oracle_first_option
			}
			add_country_modifier = { 
				name = "morale_boost"
				duration = 2000
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = oracle_war
				has_country_flag = oracle_bad_advice
				has_country_flag = oracle_first_option
			}
			add_country_modifier = { 
				name = "decreased_morale"
				duration = 2000
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = oracle_general
				has_country_flag = oracle_good_advice
				has_country_flag = oracle_first_option
			}
			create_general = { 
				tradition = 50
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = oracle_general
				has_country_flag = oracle_bad_advice
			}
			create_general = { 
				tradition = 0
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = oracle_heir
				has_country_flag = oracle_bad_advice
				has_country_flag = oracle_first_option
			}
			add_country_modifier = { 
				name = "low_fertility"
				duration = 2000
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = oracle_invest
				has_country_flag = oracle_good_advice
				has_country_flag = oracle_first_option
			}
			add_country_modifier = { 
				name = "trade_investment"
				duration = 2000
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = oracle_invest
				has_country_flag = oracle_bad_advice
				has_country_flag = oracle_first_option
			}
			add_dip_power = -100
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = oracle_war
				has_country_flag = oracle_bad_advice
				has_country_flag = oracle_second_option
			}
			add_country_modifier = { 
				name = "deserters"
				duration = 2000
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = oracle_general
				has_country_flag = oracle_good_advice
				has_country_flag = oracle_second_option
			}
			create_general = { 
				tradition = 75
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = oracle_heir
				has_country_flag = oracle_good_advice
				has_country_flag = oracle_second_option
			}
			define_heir = { 
				dynasty = ROOT
				claim = 100
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = oracle_heir
				has_country_flag = oracle_bad_advice
				has_country_flag = oracle_second_option
			}
			define_heir = { 
				dynasty = ROOT
				claim = 0
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = oracle_invest
				has_country_flag = oracle_bad_advice
				has_country_flag = oracle_second_option
			}
			add_country_modifier = { 
				name = "financial_disaster"
				duration = 2000
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = oracle_peace
				has_country_flag = oracle_good_advice
				has_country_flag = oracle_second_option
			}
			hidden_effect = { 
				change_variable = { 
					which = ahf
					value = 600
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						AND = { 
							check_variable = { 
								which = ahf
								value = 1200
							}
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							stability = 3
						}
						set_variable = { 
							which = ahf
							value = 1200
						}
					}
					else = { 
						subtract_variable = { 
							which = ahf
							value = 1200
						}
						add_stability = 1
					}
				}
				else_if = { 
					limit = { 
						NOT = { 
							AND = { 
								check_variable = { 
									which = ahf
									value = 0
								}
							}
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							NOT = { 
								stability = -2
							}
						}
						set_variable = { 
							which = ahf
							value = 0
						}
					}
					else = { 
						change_variable = { 
							which = ahf
							value = 1200
						}
						add_stability = -1
					}
				}
				set_variable = { 
					which = ahd
					which = ahf
				}
				divide_variable = { 
					which = ahd
					value = 12
				}
				multiply_variable = { 
					which = ahd
					value = 0.1
				}
				multiply_variable = { 
					which = ahd
					value = 10
				}
				set_variable = { 
					which = lsc
					value = 100
				}
				subtract_variable = { 
					which = lsc
					which = ahd
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = POP_StabAdd50
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					is_emperor_of_china = yes
				}
				add_mandate = 2.5
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = oracle_peace
				has_country_flag = oracle_bad_advice
				has_country_flag = oracle_second_option
			}
			add_country_modifier = { 
				name = "disorder"
				duration = 2000
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			clr_country_flag = oracle_war
			clr_country_flag = oracle_general
			clr_country_flag = oracle_heir
			clr_country_flag = oracle_invest
			clr_country_flag = oracle_peace
			clr_country_flag = oracle_good_advice
			clr_country_flag = oracle_bad_advice
			clr_country_flag = oracle_first_option
			clr_country_flag = oracle_second_option
		}
	}
}
province_event = { 
	id = DG_Hellenic.006
	title = "DG_Hellenic.006.title"
	desc = "DG_Hellenic.006.desc"
	picture = all_ruined_temple
	trigger = { 
		owner = { 
			religion_group = european_pagan
		}
		has_owner_religion = no
		AND = { 
			base_production = 5
		}
		NOT = { 
			has_province_flag = ancient_pagan_temple
		}
		NOT = { 
			any_neighbor_province = { 
				has_province_flag = ancient_pagan_temple
			}
		}
		OR = { 
			has_owner_culture = yes
			AND = { 
				owner = { 
					religion = hellenic_pagan
				}
				province_group = roman_dejure_group
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		years = 20
	}
	immediate = { 
		set_province_flag = ancient_pagan_temple
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				owner = { 
					has_country_flag = temple_restoration
				}
